 1 sitambar ko greenpis ne ek bollywood poster dizin kii pratiyogita kii ghoshnaa kii, jisamen kuch mashhoor filmon ko mjedaar dhang se pesh kiya gaya tha

 darasal, modi sarkaar ke satta main aane ke baad 13,700 bhartiya or videshi enjio ke epasiare licenson ko radd kiya gaya he

 inamen kai nirarthak sawaal bhi hai
 For example, why were the signatures of attendance at its annual general meeting not given to officials? How does Greenpeace International control Greenpeace India? Why does foreign income declared under FCRA not match Indian income shown in the registration department? In response to this last question, Vinuta Gopal, the interim co-executive director of Greenpeace India, says that the reason for this is clear, both the incomes were derived from two different sources, foreign and Indian respectively
